If you could throw the lid off every duck blind, stop by every pheasant field and check out every tract of timber where deer and turkey are hunted, youd probably see more Model 870 Express pumps than any other shotgun. Its been the standard for slide-action performance for more than 50 years.</font></p> <p><font size="3">Its versatility, reliability and uncompromising quality make the Model 870 Express a shotgun you cant afford to be without. The Model 870 Express Synthetic is an excellent choice as a permanent camp shotgun or as the foundation for your own personalized design. I take great care of my guns and somehow this 870 developed rust all over the front sight. I was ticked but sanded it off. I have to re-lube this thing every 2 months, it dries up quick. Or anytime this thing gets touched by bare skin you have to lube it. At least this is my experience. There is no plug in the magazine, I checked. And, this is with 2 3/4" shells too. Once you put the 5th round in the mag there is NO MORE room, not even an 8th of an inch. I don't get it. Thought about trimming the mag spring but have just left it alone. And yes it's the extended magazine, just like the one pictured. It goes out even with the end of the barrel. If the 870 is your shotgun, this is a nice HD style shotty. But, in hindsight I think I would have passed. I have a few Mossbergs and I think I will buy one of their HD shotguns as well.
